Please note that Singularity will be kept inaccessible except for specific testing windows, and may fall significantly behind Tranquility in patches. The Tranquility/Singularity diff (homepage) may not be particularly useful for the time being. Refer to the latest Tranquility patches instead.

91775 - Dragoon Navy Issue In YC128, in response to rising military conflict, the Amarr Navy commissioned the development of a specialized destroyer. With growing unrest along the borders and rising conflict with the Minmatar, the Navy required a versatile ship for both military engagements and enforcing Imperial authority.

The result was the Dragoon Navy issue, a vessel that combines the Dragoon's ability to neutralize and disable with improved missile and laser combat capabilities. A true symbol of imperial might that can be swiftly deployed wherever the Empress requires.		 Destroyer

91849 - Algos Navy Issue The election of Alix Moreau in YC128 brought a new focus on research and development to the Gallente Federation. In their role as a science advisor prior to winning the election, Moreau had tagged a number of innovative new patents submitted by CreoDron for further development. As President, they were able to ensure they entered production.

The Algos was identified as an ideal design to iterate from. Superior weapon systems, web-drone linkages, and a tougher shell were just some of the systemic improvements integrated into the new Navy Issue variant.		 Destroyer

91857 - Corax Navy Issue Following the handing over the adminstration of Jita to CONCORD in YC128, the Caldari State needed its people to rally around a new symbol of strength to help reassert its dominance following the loss of such an iconic system.

The iconic Corax was selected for a new and improved military variant that could lead the charge against the Gallente, a symbol that the Caldari could rally behind. With more robust shields, greater flexibility of fitting, and significant improvements to the explosive force of its attacks, the Corax Navy Issue is the very best of classical Caldari excellence. 91858 - Talwar Fleet Issue YC128 was a prosperous time for the Thukker tribes of the Great Wildlands. In order to protect the influx of wealth from newly discovered Phased Fields, they voted to support an increase in Republic Fleet spending.

One of the results of that spending was the development of a new Fleet Issue Talwar. Designed with assistance from Thukker engineers, the ship combines the stalwart fortitude of Fleet Issue vessels with the flexibility and efficiency that has made the caravans of the Great Wildlands uncontested within their homespace. 91863 - Dragoon Navy Issue Corporation Emblem Emblems by Paragon bring new light to your ship personalization.

By accessing your registered identity data, these nanoholographic projections emblazon your favorite vessels with symbols that matter to you. And now, by utilizing the latest in cloud-based AI synchronization, emblems remain stable even during warp.

Visit your nearest IRIS and take part in Paragon's latest initiatives to unlock new emblems today.

Paragon; be more.

WARNING: Emblems are auto-injected on purchases and cannot be transferred or traded between capsuleers. The Paragon corporation accepts no liability for failed transfer attempts.		 Ship Emblems

91910 - Military Campaign Expert System <font size="14">Navy Destroyers Expert System </font>

This Expert System makes available skills enabling a capsuleer to fly all four of the new Navy Faction Destroyers that have recently become available to capsuleers, in addition to the four existing ones. This is a promotional Expert System released to celebrate the launch of Military Campaigns.

The temporary skills provided by this Expert System last for four days.

An Expert System is a remote, restricted artificial intelligence providing you with access to certain skills during the active rental period. As it is independent from your clone and your capsule, an active Expert System is not lost on pod death or clone jump.

<font size="14">Activating an Expert System</font>

Activation of an Expert System is automatic upon redemption of the item by the specific capsuleer intending to use the service.

Expert Systems are a product developed by the PKN Interstellar consortium, made available over the HyperNet FTL communications network, and marketed by PKN Interstellar member corporations. An Expert System is a restricted AI based on artificial gelbrain technology. As the Expert System uses neural pathways based on those created by skill training or skill injection, it is compatible with capsule-ship interface and control systems. Real time command and control communication is achieved using dedicated FTL channels on PKN Interstellar's HyperNet.		 Promotional Expert Systems

1034658 Military Campaign Expert System Military Campaign Expert System Name of item 91910 (Promotional Expert Systems)
1034659 <font size="14">Navy Destroyers Expert System </font>

This Expert System makes available skills enabling a capsuleer to fly all four of the new Navy Faction Destroyers that have recently become available to capsuleers, in addition to the four existing ones. This is a promotional Expert System released to celebrate the launch of Military Campaigns.

The temporary skills provided by this Expert System last for four days.

An Expert System is a remote, restricted artificial intelligence providing you with access to certain skills during the active rental period. As it is independent from your clone and your capsule, an active Expert System is not lost on pod death or clone jump.

<font size="14">Activating an Expert System</font>

Activation of an Expert System is automatic upon redemption of the item by the specific capsuleer intending to use the service.

Expert Systems are a product developed by the PKN Interstellar consortium, made available over the HyperNet FTL communications network, and marketed by PKN Interstellar member corporations. An Expert System is a restricted AI based on artificial gelbrain technology. As the Expert System uses neural pathways based on those created by skill training or skill injection, it is compatible with capsule-ship interface and control systems. Real time command and control communication is achieved using dedicated FTL channels on PKN Interstellar's HyperNet.		 <font size="14"><b>Navy Destroyers Expert System </b></font>

This Expert System makes available skills enabling a capsuleer to fly all four of the new Navy Faction Destroyers that have recently become available to capsuleers, in addition to the four existing ones. This is a promotional Expert System released to celebrate the launch of Military Campaigns.

1039504 <font size="14">Secrets Operations Expert System</font>

This Expert System has been loaded with advanced ship operation skills, to mimic experience of an Omega capsuleer.

An Expert System is a remote, restricted artificial intelligence providing you with access to certain skills during the active 1 day rental period.
As it is independent from your clone and your capsule, an active Expert System is not lost on pod death or clone jump.

<font size="14">Activating an Expert System</font>

Activation of an Expert System is automatic upon redemption of the item by the specific capsuleer intending to use the service.

Expert Systems are a product developed by the PKN Interstellar consortium, made available over the HyperNet FTL communications network, and marketed by PKN Interstellar member corporations. An Expert System is a restricted AI based on artificial gelbrain technology. As the Expert System uses neural pathways based on those created by skill training or skill injection, it is compatible with capsule-ship interface and control systems. Real time command and control communication is achieved using dedicated FTL channels on PKN Interstellar's HyperNet.		 <font size="14">Secrets Operations Expert System</font>

Famed for their ability to establish tactical superiority even against much larger enemy fleets, the Warpath Stark are often underestimated but never outclassed.
